class=\"cycle-gradient\"></div>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"cycle-overlay\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<h3 class=\"cycle-selector-title\">Sound Foundations</h3>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"cycle-selector-description\">The Brighton campus is where it all began for BIMM, and it’s an amazing place to get your start in music too. It’s spread across three buildings, each with first-class facilities for the modern music student.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"/brighton/\" class=\"f-btn f-btn--more\">Find out more about Brighton <span>+</span></a>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"cycle-item-image panel-container\" style=\"background-image:url('https://www.bimm.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2014/08/1511AW-songwriting_bristol_01-widescreen.jpg');\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"cycle-gradient\"></div>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"cycle-overlay\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<h3 class=\"cycle-selector-title\">Lively Buzz</h3>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"cycle-selector-description\">The BIMM Bristol campus at King Square first opened its doors in 2008. There’s a lively buzz to the campus, not to mention stunning state-of-the-art facilities – making it a special place to pursue and achieve your musical ambitions.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"/bristol/\" class=\"f-btn f-btn--more\">Find out more about Bristol <span>+</span></a>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"cycle-item-image panel-container\" style=\"background-image:url('https://www.bimm.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2014/08/1510IX-eventmanagement_manchester_01-widescreen.jpg');\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"cycle-gradient\"></div>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"cycle-overlay\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<h3 class=\"cycle-selector-title\">Centre Stage</h3>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"cycle-selector-description\">With several famous live venues nearby, BIMM Manchester pitches you right into the heart of the city’s dynamic and diverse music scene. It’s our newest campus, with state-of-the-art facilities and equipment designed for modern musicianship.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"/manchester/\" class=\"f-btn f-btn--more\">Find out more about Manchester <span>+</span></a>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"cycle-item-image panel-container\" style=\"background-image:url('https://www.bimm.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2014/08/1510RY-musicbusiness_dublin_06-widescreen.jpg');\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"cycle-gradient\"></div>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"cycle-overlay\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<h3 class=\"cycle-selector-title\">Exciting Times</h3>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"cycle-selector-description\">The 7000ft<sup>2</sup> Dublin campus opened in 2011, and it quickly expanded to include a new building in the city’s historic Coombe area. With big plans for the new facility, it’s an exciting place to be right now – and a superb environment to carve out a career in music.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"/dublin/\" class=\"f-btn f-btn--more\">Find out more about Dublin <span>+</span></a>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"cycle-item-image panel-container\" style=\"background-image:url('https://www.bimm.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2014/08/1510BF-guitar_london_04-widescreen.jpg');\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"cycle-gradient\"></div>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"cycle-overlay\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<h3 class=\"cycle-selector-title\">Industry Experience</h3>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"cycle-selector-description\">After 30 years in Acton, BIMM London (previously known as Tech Music School) moved to a stunning new facility in Fulham in 2013. The new five-storey building provides 19,000ft<sup>2</sup> of studios and study rooms in the world’s music capital.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"/london/\" class=\"f-btn f-btn--more\">Find out more about London <span>+</span></a>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"cycle-item-image panel-container\" style=\"background-image:url('https://www.bimm.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2015/01/1130NS-img_4159-widescreen.jpg');\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"cycle-gradient\"></div>\n\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"cycle-overlay\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<h3 class=\"cycle-selector-title\">Historic Move</h3>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"cycle-selector-description\">BIMM Berlin shares a facility with our partners, Noisy Academy, in the artistic Friedrichshain-Kreuzberg district. The building provides state-of-the-art professional facilities, including top-of-the-range Mac suites, backline-fitted rehearsal studios, and an independently owned recording studio.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"/berlin/\" class=\"f-btn f-btn--more\">Find out more about Berlin <span>+</span></a>\n\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\n\t</div>\n\n</div>\n    </div>\n</section>\n\n<section class=\"section--dark\" id=\"page-tutors\">\n    <div class=\"f-row\">\n        <div class=\"panel-split--right panel-split-tutor \">\n\n    <div class=\"f-33 panel-container\"><div class=\"container-intro     \" style=\"background-image:url('');\">\n\n    <!-- LOCATION OWNERSHIP -->\n    \n    <!-- Tag -->\n            <p class=\"tag-block\">The best connected:</p>\n    \n    <!-- Title -->\n            <h4>BIMM Tutors</h4>\n    \n    <!-- Intro text -->\n            \n                    <p></p><p>With years of experience in the music industry, our tutors have achieved a lot. They’ve toured the world, scored multi-platinum hit records, interviewed global superstars, organised major music festivals, and collaborated with some of the world’s most incredible acts, including Oasis, Prince, Rolling Stones, Beyonce and Sir Paul McCartney.
